- **Dependencies (outgoing):** 0 — _(none found by label-scan)_
- **Used by (incoming):** 4 — [`GLC2:corollary:c:sigma and Sat`](./GLC2.md#glc2-corollary-c-sigma-and-sat-1b7c3ba7), [`GLC2:remark:auto0020@L2244`](./GLC2.md#glc2-remark-auto0020-l2244-2462cbf1), [`GLC2:remark:auto0121@L9097`](./GLC2.md#glc2-remark-auto0121-l9097-9a476580), [`GLC2:remark:r:CS again`](./GLC2.md#glc2-remark-r-cs-again-2e101270)

```tex

```

- **Claim ID:** `GLC2:remark:auto0024@L2583`
- **Location:** `gaits2.tex` lines 2583-2590
- **Context:** Geometric Satake and Casselman-Shalika formula: recollections
- **Dependencies (outgoing):** 0 — _(none found by label-scan)_
- **Used by (incoming):** 0 — _(none)_

```tex

```

- **Used by (incoming):** 1 — [`GLC2:corollary:c:geom Sat tau`](./GLC2.md#glc2-corollary-c-geom-sat-tau-c3c28dc2)

```tex
\label{c:sigma and Sat} The following diagram of anti-equivalences commutes: $$ \CD \Sph_G @>{\Sat_G}>> \Sph_\cG^{\on{spec}} \\ @V{\sigma}VV \\ \Sph_G & & @VV{\sigma^{\on{spec}}}V \\ @V{\tau_G}VV \\ \Sph_G @>{\Sat_G}>> \Sph_\cG^{\on{spec}}. \endCD $$
```

- **Location:** `gaits2.tex` lines 24690-24694
- **Context:** Factorization patterns
- **Dependencies (outgoing):** 0 — _(none found by label-scan)_

```tex
\label{l:act t} Under the above circumstances, the category $L\mod(\bC) := L\mod(\bC') \underset{\bC'}\times \bC$ (resp., $A\mod(\bC) := A\mod(\bC') \underset{\bC'}\times \bC$) admits a unique t-structure for which the forgetful functor to $\bC$ is t-exact.
```
